]]>tag:localist.com,2008:EventInstance_4948970749160425.790444-80.132148Thu, 29 May 2025 00:00:00 -04002025-05-29T00:00:00-04:00https://calendar.fiu.edu/event/creole-archive-project-polone-nwa-constitution-1805-exhibition-by-dr-jacek-kolasinskiArts & CultureExhibitionsMay 29, 2025: Language, Culture, and Society in Havana in 1830 at GL - Green LibraryDictionaries and encyclopedias from Europe inspired a group of intellectuals in Havana to compile the typical voices of Cuba around 1830. This effort resulted in a vocabulary that remained unpublished for 190 years, until Dr. ChÃ¡vez-Rivera edited and published it in 2021. The original manuscript circulated in the XIX century and was an influence on the island and abroad. The objective of this conference is to identify particularities of that interest in the Spanish language and the inclination for lexicographic activity in Cuba in the years prior to the appearance of Esteban Pichardoâ€™s Diccionario provincial de voces cubanas in 1836. This conference reconstructs the creative and bibliographic environment of that pioneering group in 1830 who had the good sense to work as a team, recognize aspects of Cuban identity, and capture the various voices and phrases used by their contemporaries on the island. 
GUEST SPEAKER: Dr. Armando ChÃ¡vez-Rivera. Associate Professor and Director of the Spanish Program at the University of Houston-Victoria, Texas, and a Scholar in Residence at the Kluge Center at the Library of Congress. Member of the North American Academy of the Spanish Language.
This event is co-sponsored by the Kimberly Green Latin America and Caribbean Center and FIU Libraries. This event is made possible with the support of LACC's Department of Education Title VI Grant. This event is free and open to the public. This event will be conducted in Spanish. To confirm your in-person attendance, please write or call (305) 348â€“1991.
[View on site](https://calendar.fiu.edu/event/language-culture-and-society-in-havana-in-1830-3028) |

As recommended in our Equity Action Initiative, FIU seeks to align with the spirit of this holiday, to make Juneteenth an official day of observance at Florida International University. Additionally, we stand in support of the Student Government Association of Florida. 
The theme for FIU first inaugural Juneteenth celebration is â€œEducate, Celebrate, and Healâ€. Educating, celebrating, and embracing the truths of Juneteenth can serve to expand the collective knowledge of our entire FIU community and accelerate an appreciation for the Black history excluded from pedagogy, that may have framed a different America. Celebrating Juneteenth complements the work of the Founding Fathers, being the architects of the Declaration of Independence, and brings to the conversation, the 400 years Blacks have tried to achieve equality in enjoying â€˜life, liberty and the pursuit of happinessâ€™. During this week of observance, we will provide programming and activities to commemorate Juneteenth beginning June 14 and culminating with a Juneteenth Freedom Day Celebration on Saturday, June 19 from 10am to 4pm. To learn more about this celebration, visit <https://ace.fiu.edu/juneteenth/>

<item>
<title>May 29, 2025: Language, Culture, and Society in Havana in 1830 at GL - Green Library</title>
<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>Dictionaries and encyclopedias from Europe inspired a group of intellectuals in Havana to compile the typical voices of Cuba around 1830. This effort resulted in a vocabulary that remained unpublished for 190 years, until Dr. ChÃ¡vez-Rivera edited and published it in 2021. The original manuscript circulated in the XIX century and was an influence on the island and abroad. The objective of this conference is to identify particularities of that interest in the Spanish language and the inclination for lexicographic activity in Cuba in the years prior to the appearance of Esteban Pichardoâ€™s Diccionario provincial de voces cubanas in 1836. This conference reconstructs the creative and bibliographic environment of that pioneering group in 1830 who had the good sense to work as a team, recognize aspects of Cuban identity, and capture the various voices and phrases used by their contemporaries on the island. </p> <p> </p> <p>GUEST SPEAKER: Dr. Armando ChÃ¡vez-Rivera. Associate Professor and Director of the Spanish Program at the University of Houston-Victoria, Texas, and a Scholar in Residence at the Kluge Center at the Library of Congress. Member of the North American Academy of the Spanish Language.</p> <p> </p> <p>This event is co-sponsored by the Kimberly Green Latin America and Caribbean Center and FIU Libraries. This event is made possible with the support of LACC's Department of Education Title VI Grant. This event is free and open to the public. This event will be conducted in Spanish. To confirm your in-person attendance, please write <a href="mailto:cri@fiu.edu">cri@fiu.edu</a> or call (305) 348â€“1991.</p> <p><a href="https://calendar.fiu.edu/event/language-culture-and-society-in-havana-in-1830-3028">View on site</a> | <a href="mailto:?subject=I+found+an+interesting+event%3A+Language%2C+Culture%2C+and+Society+in+Havana+in+1830&amp;body=I+found+an+interesting+event+you+may+like%3A%0A%0A%0ADate%3A+May+29%2C+2025%0A%0ADescription%3A%0ADictionaries+and+encyclopedias+from+Europe+inspired+a+group+of+intellectuals+in+Havana+to+compile+the+typical+voices+of+Cuba+around+1830.+This+effort+resulted+in+a+vocabulary+that+remained+unpublished+for+190+years%2C+until+Dr.+Ch%C3%A1vez-Rivera+edited+and+published+it+in+2021.+The+original+manuscript+circulated+in+the+XIX+century+and+was+an+influence+on+the+island+and+abroad.+The+objective+of+this+conference+is+to+identify+particularities+of+that+interest+in+the+Spanish+language+and+the+inclination+for+lexicographic+activity+in+Cuba+in+the+years+prior+to+the+appearance+of+Esteban+Pichardo%E2%80%99s+Diccionario+provincial+de+voces+cubanas+in+1836.+This+conference+reconstructs+the+creative+and+bibliographic+environment+of+that+pioneering+group+in+1830+who+had+the+good+sense+to+work+as+a+team%2C+recognize+aspects+of+Cuban+identity%2C+and+capture+the+various+voices+and+phrases+used+by+their+contemporaries+on+the+island.++%0A%0A+%0A%0AGUEST+SPEAKER%3A+Dr.+Armando+Ch%C3%A1vez-Rivera.+Associate+Professor+and+Director+of+the+Spanish+Program+at+the+University+of+Houston-Victoria%2C+Texas%2C+and+a+Scholar+in+Residence+at+the+Kluge+Center+at+the+Library+of+Congress.+Member+of+the+North+American+Academy+of+the+Spanish+Language.%0A%0A+%0A%0AThis+event+is+co-sponsored+by+the+Kimberly+Green+Latin+America+and+Caribbean+Center+and+FIU+Libraries.+This+event+is+made+possible+with+the+support+of+LACC%27s+Department+of+Education+Title+VI+Grant.+This+event+is+free+and+open+to+the+public.++This+event+will+be+conducted+in+Spanish.+To+confirm+your+in-person+attendance%2C+please+write+cri%40fiu.edu+or+call+%28305%29+348%E2%80%931991.%0A%0Ahttps%3A%2F%2Fcalendar.fiu.edu%2Fevent%2Flanguage-culture-and-society-in-havana-in-1830-3028%0A">Email <title>Jun 3, 2025: 2025 Global Forensic Science Symposium at MARC - Management & Advanced Research</title>
<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>The 2025 Global Forensic Science Symposium will present ground-breaking forensic science research from 40 experts worldwide. Our theme this year is Collaboration in Forensic Scienceâ€”an essential practice to advance the disciplines across campus and around the world.</p> <p>Presentation topics include: Medico-Legal Death Investigation, DNA, Genetic Genealogy, Toxicology, Canine Sensors, Illicit Drug Trade, Contamination Detection, Trace Evidence, Nanotechnology, Explosives, Crime Scene Photography, Chemical Analysis, Quantification, Fingerprint Development, Digital and Crypto Forensics, Mass Disaster Victim Management, Firearms, Accreditation, Certification, and Laboratory Operations.</p> <p>Schedule: <br />Tuesday, June 3: In-person, MARC 290, and live-streamed online <br />Wednesday &amp; Thursday, June 4 &amp; 5: Livestream only</p> <p>Whether you attend in-person or virtually - registration is FREE! <item>
<title>Jun 19, 2025: FIU Celebrates Juneteenth</title>
<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>Juneteenth celebrates African American freedom and achievement, while encouraging continuous self-development. As recommended in our Equity Action Initiative, FIU seeks to align with the spirit of this holiday, to make Juneteenth an official day of observance at Florida International University. Additionally, we stand in support of the Student Government Association of Florida.</p> <p>The theme for FIU first inaugural Juneteenth celebration is â€œEducate, Celebrate, and Healâ€. Educating, celebrating, and embracing the truths of Juneteenth can serve to expand the collective knowledge of our entire FIU community and accelerate an appreciation for the Black history excluded from pedagogy, that may have framed a different America. Celebrating Juneteenth complements the work of the Founding Fathers, being the architects of the Declaration of Independence, and brings to the conversation, the 400 years Blacks have tried to achieve equality in enjoying â€˜life, liberty and the pursuit of happinessâ€™. During this week of observance, we will provide programming and activities to commemorate Juneteenth beginning June 14 and culminating with a Juneteenth Freedom Day Celebration on Saturday, June 19 from 10am to 4pm. To learn more about this celebration, visit <a href="https://ace.fiu.edu/juneteenth/">https://ace.fiu.edu/juneteenth/</a></p> <p><a href="https://calendar.fiu.edu/event/fiu_celebrates_juneteenth">View on site</a> | <a href="mailto:?subject=I+found+an+interesting+event%3A+FIU+Celebrates+Juneteenth&amp;body=I+found+an+interesting+event+you+may+like%3A%0A%0A%0ADate%3A+Jun+19%2C+2025%0A%0ADescription%3A%0AJuneteenth+celebrates+African+American+freedom+and+achievement%2C+while+encouraging+continuous+self-development.+As+recommended+in+our+Equity+Action+Initiative%2C+FIU+seeks+to+align+with+the+spirit+of+this+holiday%2C+to+make+Juneteenth+an+official+day+of+observance+at+Florida+International+University.+Additionally%2C+we+stand+in+support+of+the+Student+Government+Association+of+Florida.%0A%0AThe+theme+for+FIU+first+inaugural+Juneteenth+celebration+is+%E2%80%9CEducate%2C+Celebrate%2C+and+Heal%E2%80%9D.+Educating%2C+celebrating%2C+and+embracing+the+truths+of+Juneteenth+can+serve+to+expand+the+collective+knowledge+of+our+entire+FIU+community+and+accelerate+an+appreciation+for+the+Black+history+excluded+from+pedagogy%2C+that+may+have+framed+a+different+America.+Celebrating+Juneteenth+complements+the+work+of+the+Founding+Fathers%2C+being+the+architects+of+the+Declaration+of+Independence%2C+and+brings+to+the+conversation%2C+the+400+years+Blacks+have+tried+to+achieve+equality+in+enjoying+%E2%80%98life%2C+liberty+and+the+pursuit+of+happiness%E2%80%99.+During+this+week+of+observance%2C+we+will+provide+programming+and+activities+to+commemorate+Juneteenth+beginning+June+14+and+culminating+with+a+Juneteenth+Freedom+Day+Celebration+on+Saturday%2C+June+19+from+10am+to+4pm.+To+learn+more+about+this+celebration%2C+visit+https%3A%2F%2Face.fiu.edu%2Fjuneteenth%2F%0A%0Ahttps%3A%2F%2Fcalendar.fiu.edu%2Fevent%2Ffiu_celebrates_juneteenth%0A">Email this event</a></p> ]]>
